    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue

                    onerror(os.open, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                else:

                            except OSError:

                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                            dirfd_closed = True

topfd = 17, path = '/tmp/tmp48xr0uoe/sessions/test_session_pure_text'
onerror = <function TemporaryDirectory._rmtree.<locals>.onerror at 0x7fccd4f25120>

    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue

                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())

                                raise OSError("Cannot call rmtree on a symbolic "
                                              "link")

                                onerror(os.path.islink, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                    finally:

    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue
            if is_dir:
                try:
                    dirfd = os.open(entry.name, os.O_RDONLY | os.O_NONBLOCK, dir_fd=topfd)
                    dirfd_closed = False
                except OSError:
                    onerror(os.open, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                else:
                    try:
                        if os.path.samestat(orig_st, os.fstat(dirfd)):
                            _rmtree_safe_fd(dirfd, fullname, onerror)
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                # close() should not be retried after an error.
                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                            dirfd_closed = True
                            try:
                                os.rmdir(entry.name, dir_fd=topfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.rmdir, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        else:
                            try:
                                # This can only happen if someone replaces
                                # a directory with a symlink after the call to
                                # os.scandir or stat.S_ISDIR above.
                                raise OSError("Cannot call rmtree on a symbolic "
                                              "link")
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.path.islink, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                    finally:
                        if not dirfd_closed:
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
            else:

    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue
            if is_dir:
                try:
                    dirfd = os.open(entry.name, os.O_RDONLY | os.O_NONBLOCK, dir_fd=topfd)
                    dirfd_closed = False
                except OSError:
                    onerror(os.open, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                else:
                    try:
                        if os.path.samestat(orig_st, os.fstat(dirfd)):
                            _rmtree_safe_fd(dirfd, fullname, onerror)
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                # close() should not be retried after an error.
                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                            dirfd_closed = True
                            try:
                                os.rmdir(entry.name, dir_fd=topfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.rmdir, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        else:
                            try:

                                # a directory with a symlink after the call to
                                # os.scandir or stat.S_ISDIR above.
                                raise OSError("Cannot call rmtree on a symbolic "
                                              "link")
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.path.islink, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                    finally:
                        if not dirfd_closed:
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:

    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue
            if is_dir:
                try:
                    dirfd = os.open(entry.name, os.O_RDONLY | os.O_NONBLOCK, dir_fd=topfd)
                    dirfd_closed = False
                except OSError:
                    onerror(os.open, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                else:
                    try:
                        if os.path.samestat(orig_st, os.fstat(dirfd)):
                            _rmtree_safe_fd(dirfd, fullname, onerror)
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                # close() should not be retried after an error.
                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                            dirfd_closed = True
                            try:
                                os.rmdir(entry.name, dir_fd=topfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.rmdir, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        else:

                                # a directory with a symlink after the call to
                                # os.scandir or stat.S_ISDIR above.
                                raise OSError("Cannot call rmtree on a symbolic "
                                              "link")
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.path.islink, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                    finally:
                        if not dirfd_closed:

    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue
            if is_dir:
                try:
                    dirfd = os.open(entry.name, os.O_RDONLY | os.O_NONBLOCK, dir_fd=topfd)
                    dirfd_closed = False
                except OSError:
                    onerror(os.open, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                else:
                    try:
                        if os.path.samestat(orig_st, os.fstat(dirfd)):
                            _rmtree_safe_fd(dirfd, fullname, onerror)
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                # close() should not be retried after an error.
                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                            dirfd_closed = True
                            try:
                                os.rmdir(entry.name, dir_fd=topfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.rmdir, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        else:
                            try:
                                # This can only happen if someone replaces
                                # a directory with a symlink after the call to
                                # os.scandir or stat.S_ISDIR above.
                                raise OSError("Cannot call rmtree on a symbolic "
                                              "link")
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.path.islink, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                    finally:
                        if not dirfd_closed:

                                os.close(dirfd)

        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:

            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:

            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:

                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue

    def _rmtree_safe_fd(topfd, path, onerror):
        try:
            with os.scandir(topfd) as scandir_it:
                entries = list(scandir_it)
        except OSError as err:
            err.filename = path
            onerror(os.scandir, path, sys.exc_info())
            return
        for entry in entries:
            fullname = os.path.join(path, entry.name)
            try:
                is_dir = entry.is_dir(follow_symlinks=False)
            except OSError:
                is_dir = False
            else:
                if is_dir:
                    try:
                        orig_st = entry.stat(follow_symlinks=False)
                        is_dir = stat.S_ISDIR(orig_st.st_mode)
                    except OSError:
                        onerror(os.lstat, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        continue
            if is_dir:
                try:
                    dirfd = os.open(entry.name, os.O_RDONLY | os.O_NONBLOCK, dir_fd=topfd)
                    dirfd_closed = False
                except OSError:
                    onerror(os.open, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                else:
                    try:
                        if os.path.samestat(orig_st, os.fstat(dirfd)):
                            _rmtree_safe_fd(dirfd, fullname, onerror)
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                # close() should not be retried after an error.
                                dirfd_closed = True
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                            dirfd_closed = True
                            try:
                                os.rmdir(entry.name, dir_fd=topfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.rmdir, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                        else:
                            try:
                                # This can only happen if someone replaces
                                # a directory with a symlink after the call to
                                # os.scandir or stat.S_ISDIR above.
                                raise OSError("Cannot call rmtree on a symbolic "
                                              "link")
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.path.islink, fullname, sys.exc_info())
                    finally:
                        if not dirfd_closed:
                            try:
                                os.close(dirfd)
                            except OSError:
                                onerror(os.close, fullname, sys.exc_info())
            else:
